Private Sub btnReadFile_Click()

'''''On Error GoTo Err_btnReadFile_Click

SV01Max = 0
SV02Max = 0
SV03Max = 0
SV04Max = 0
SV05Max = 0
SV06Max = 0
SV07Max = 0
SV08Max = 0
SV09Max = 0
SV10Max = 0
SV01Min = 1
SV02Min = 1
SV03Min = 1
SV04Min = 1
SV05Min = 1
SV06Min = 1
SV07Min = 1
SV08Min = 1
SV09Min = 1
SV10Min = 1
SV01Tot = 0
SV02Tot = 0
SV03Tot = 0
SV04Tot = 0
SV05Tot = 0
SV06Tot = 0
SV07Tot = 0
SV08Tot = 0
SV09Tot = 0
SV10Tot = 0
importCSV = ""
Form_DIM_TEST_10.hiddenCSVFileLocation = ""
Form_DIM_TEST_10.HiddenCSVTestSystem = ""
Form_DIM_TEST_10.hiddenCSVSaveLocation = ""

TestSampleNo = 1
TestSampleColumn = 1

'Get all import file locations
Dim fileLocations As Variant
fileLocations = QueryToArray("select ImpFileLoc,TestSystem,SaveFileLoc from ImpFileLocTbl")

'Make sure a list of file locations came back.
If isArrayEmpty(fileLocations) = False Then

    Set FE = CreateObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject")
    
    'Find out which CSV file will be picked up
    For j = LBound(fileLocations) To UBound(fileLocations) - 1
        csvfile = fileLocations(j, 0)
        csvTestSystem = fileLocations(j, 1)
        csvSaveFileLocation = fileLocations(j, 2)
        
        If FE.FileExists(csvfile) And importCSV = "" Then
            importCSV = csvfile
            Form_DIM_TEST_10.hiddenCSVFileLocation = importCSV
            Form_DIM_TEST_10.HiddenCSVTestSystem = csvTestSystem
            Form_DIM_TEST_10.hiddenCSVSaveLocation = csvSaveFileLocation
            
         ElseIf FE.FileExists(csvfile) And importCSV <> "" Then
            MsgBox "There is a CSV file in in multiple directories."
            Exit Sub
         End If
    Next
    

    
    'If we don't have a file an import CSV file we need to exit.
     If importCSV = "" Then
        MsgBox "No CSV file found"
        Exit Sub
     End If
Else
     MsgBox "Unable to obtain list of CSV directories. Please have an administrator look at this issue."
     Exit Sub
End If




If importCSV <> "" Then

'If this is an Inspec file cutoff the first column and replace spaces ,,,, with -999
csvTestSystem = Form_DIM_TEST_10.HiddenCSVTestSystem

If csvTestSystem = "Inspec" Then
    If TextFile_FindReplace(importCSV, ",,,,", ",-999,-999,-999,-999") = False Then
        MsgBox "There was a problem manipulating Inspec file."
        Exit Sub
    End If
End If

Open importCSV For Input As #1
Do While Not EOF(1)                         ' Loop until end of file.

If (TestSampleColumn = 1) And (TestSampleColumn <= TestColumn) And Not EOF(1) Then
Call TestSamp1
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T1HI.Value = SV01Max
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T1LOW.Value = SV01Min
End If
If (TestSampleColumn = 2) And (TestSampleColumn <= TestColumn) And Not EOF(1) Then
Call TestSamp2
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T2HI.Value = SV02Max
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T2LOW.Value = SV02Min
End If
If (TestSampleColumn = 3) And (TestSampleColumn <= TestColumn) And Not EOF(1) Then
Call TestSamp3
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T3HI.Value = SV03Max
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T3LOW.Value = SV03Min
End If
If (TestSampleColumn = 4) And (TestSampleColumn <= TestColumn) And Not EOF(1) Then
Call TestSamp4
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T4HI.Value = SV04Max
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T4LOW.Value = SV04Min
End If
If (TestSampleColumn = 5) And (TestSampleColumn <= TestColumn) And Not EOF(1) Then
Call TestSamp5
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T5HI.Value = SV05Max
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T5LOW.Value = SV05Min
End If
If (TestSampleColumn = 6) And (TestSampleColumn <= TestColumn) And Not EOF(1) Then
Call TestSamp6
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T6HI.Value = SV06Max
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T6LOW.Value = SV06Min
End If
If (TestSampleColumn = 7) And (TestSampleColumn <= TestColumn) And Not EOF(1) Then
Call TestSamp7
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T7HI.Value = SV07Max
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T7LOW.Value = SV07Min
End If
If (TestSampleColumn = 8) And (TestSampleColumn <= TestColumn) And Not EOF(1) Then
Call TestSamp8
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T8HI.Value = SV08Max
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T8LOW.Value = SV08Min
End If
If (TestSampleColumn = 9) And (TestSampleColumn <= TestColumn) And Not EOF(1) Then
Call TestSamp9
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T9HI.Value = SV09Max
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T9LOW.Value = SV09Min
End If
If (TestSampleColumn = 10) And (TestSampleColumn <= TestColumn) And Not EOF(1) Then
Call TestSamp10
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T10HI.Value = SV10Max
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T10LOW.Value = SV10Min
End If

If TestSampleNo < TestCount1 Then
TestSampleNo = TestSampleNo + 1
End If
TestSampleColumn = 1

Loop
'Close #1    ' Close file.

If 1 <= TestColumn Then
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T1AVG.Value = (SV01Tot / TestCount1)
End If

If 2 <= TestColumn Then
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T2AVG.Value = (SV02Tot / TestCount1)
End If

End If

If 6 <= TestColumn Then

End If

If 7 <= TestColumn Then

End If

If 8 <= TestColumn Then

End If

End If

If 10 <= TestColumn Then
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T10AVG.Value = (SV10Tot / TestCount1)
End If

        Form_DIM_TEST_10.btnRecal.Visible = True
        Form_DIM_TEST_10.btnSave.Visible = True
        Form_DIM_TEST_10.btnSave.SetFocus
        Form_DIM_TEST_10.btnReadFile.Visible = False

End If
    
Close #1    ' Close file.

If Test_Order_EM = 1 Then

End If

Private Sub TestSamp1()
    
If TestSampleColumn <= TestColumn Then

    Input #1, RawStringData                 ' Read data into variable.

    TrimedData = Val(Trim(RawStringData))
        
    If ((TestSampleNo = 1) And (TrimedData = 0) And Not EOF(1)) Or (csvTestSystem = "Inspec" And Not EOF(1)) Then
        Input #1, RawStringData                 ' Read data into variable.
        TrimedData = Val(Trim(RawStringData))
    End If
    
    If (TestSampleNo > 1) And (TrimedData = 0) Then
        GoTo GetNextReading
    End If
   
    If TrimedData > SV01Max Then
        SV01Max = TrimedData
    End If
    If TrimedData < SV01Min Then
        SV01Min = TrimedData
    End If
    
    SV01Tot = SV01Tot + TrimedData
    
    If TestSampleNo <= TestCount1 Then
        ReadingValue(1, TestSampleNo) = TrimedData
        'Form_DIM_TEST_10.txtS0101.Value = TrimedData
    End If

GetNextReading:

TestSampleColumn = TestSampleColumn + 1
End If

End Sub

Private Sub btnSave_Click()
'On Error GoTo Err_btnSave_Click
With CodeContextObject

Dim StartTime As Double
Debug.Print String(65535, vbCr)
StartTime = Timer

Dim TD, MD, MDN, PN, RN, RLN, MN, TN, EI, en, TA, TR
Dim LT1, LT2, LT3, LT4, LT5, LT6, LT7, LT8, LT9, LT10
Dim Ma1, Ma2, Ma3, Ma4, Ma5, Ma6, Ma7, Ma8, Ma9, Ma10
Dim Mi1, Mi2, Mi3, Mi4, Mi5, Mi6, Mi7, Mi8, Mi9, Mi10
Dim TstPrt
Dim TestCriteria
Dim TAR

Dim GCSVLoc As String
Dim GSavLoc As String
Dim CatchTotHi As Long
Dim CatchTotLw As Long
Dim CatchTot As Long
Dim TotHi
Dim totLw
Dim TotAv
Dim NT As String
Dim TestSystem As String
TestSystem = Form_DIM_TEST_10.HiddenCSVTestSystem

'Start mouse hourglass
Screen.MousePointer = 11

'Dim XXX As String

'Add test data for save and override here
'start catch totals at 0
CatchTotHi = 0
CatchTotLw = 0
CatchTot = 0
TotHi = 0
totLw = 0

'added 3/23/16 to clear before establishing data

Catch = 0
Catch2 = 0
Catch3 = 0
Catch4 = 0
Catch5 = 0
Catch6 = 0
Catch7 = 0
Catch8 = 0
Catch9 = 0
Catch10 = 0

nCatch = 0
ncatch1 = 0
nCatch2 = 0
nCatch3 = 0
nCatch4 = 0
nCatch5 = 0
nCatch6 = 0
nCatch7 = 0
nCatch8 = 0
nCatch9 = 0
nCatch10 = 0

cCatch = 0
cCatch2 = 0
cCatch3 = 0
cCatch4 = 0
cCatch5 = 0
cCatch6 = 0
cCatch7 = 0
cCatch8 = 0
cCatch9 = 0
cCatch10 = 0

cnCatch = 0
cnCatch2 = 0
cnCatch3 = 0
cnCatch4 = 0
cnCatch5 = 0
cnCatch6 = 0
cnCatch7 = 0
cnCatch8 = 0
cnCatch9 = 0
cnCatch10 = 0

If Forms![DIM_TEST_10]![TAR5] = True And Form_DIM_TEST_10.txtS0501 = 0 Then
MsgBox "You have not entered your accepted value.", , "Stop!"
Exit Sub
ElseIf Forms![DIM_TEST_10]![TAR5] = True And Form_DIM_TEST_10.txtS0502 = 0 Then
MsgBox "You have not entered your Rejected value.", , "Stop!"
Exit Sub
End If

'Insure re-calc is done before save
Call btnRecal_Click

'Call catch tests high and low for detail section - Remove any manual Accept Rejects
If Form_DIM_TEST_10.txtS0101.Visible = True And Forms![DIM_TEST_10]![TAR1] = False Then Call MxCatch1
If Form_DIM_TEST_10.txtS0201.Visible = True And Forms![DIM_TEST_10]![TAR2] = False Then Call MxCatch2
If Form_DIM_TEST_10.txtS0301.Visible = True And Forms![DIM_TEST_10]![TAR3] = False Then Call MxCatch3
If Form_DIM_TEST_10.txtS0401.Visible = True And Forms![DIM_TEST_10]![TAR4] = False Then Call MxCatch4
If Form_DIM_TEST_10.txtS0501.Visible = True And Forms![DIM_TEST_10]![TAR5] = False Then Call MxCatch5
If Form_DIM_TEST_10.txtS0601.Visible = True And Forms![DIM_TEST_10]![TAR6] = False Then Call MxCatch6
If Form_DIM_TEST_10.txtS0701.Visible = True And Forms![DIM_TEST_10]![TAR7] = False Then Call MxCatch7
If Form_DIM_TEST_10.txtS0801.Visible = True And Forms![DIM_TEST_10]![TAR8] = False Then Call MxCatch8
If Form_DIM_TEST_10.txtS0901.Visible = True And Forms![DIM_TEST_10]![TAR9] = False Then Call MxCatch9
If Form_DIM_TEST_10.txtS1001.Visible = True And Forms![DIM_TEST_10]![TAR10] = False Then Call MxCatch10

'call catch test high and low for footer
Call MxCatchFoot

'Add catched amounts

CatchTotHi = Catch + Catch2 + Catch3 + Catch4 + Catch5 + Catch6 + Catch7 + Catch8 + Catch9 + Catch10
CatchTotLw = nCatch + nCatch2 + nCatch3 + nCatch4 + nCatch5 + nCatch6 + nCatch7 + nCatch8 + nCatch9 + nCatch10
CatchTot = CatchTotHi + CatchTotLw
TotHi = CHTH + CLTH + CATH
totLw = CHTL + CLTL + CATH

'MsgBox "Catch7: " & Catch7
'MsgBox "nCatch7: " & nCatch7

'MsgBox "TotHi: " & TotHi
'MsgBox "TotLw: " & totLw

Call btn1_10_Click

'give ablity to override

If Form_DIM_TEST_10.Check792 = 0 Then

'if no override or override not checked yet and out of spec, this message appears.

    Style = vbYesNo + vbCritical + vbDefaultButton2    ' Define buttons.

Private Sub EMP_ID_AfterUpdate()

Dim Msg, Style, Title, Response, MyString

EmpName1 = ""
VarResult = ""

EmpName1 = DLookup("[EMPLOYEENAME]", "EMPLOYEE", "[EMPLOYEEID] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!EMP_ID & "'")

VarResult = Nz(EmpName1, "NOT FOUND")

If VarResult = "NOT FOUND" Then

Msg = "Employee ID NOT Found"
Style = vbOKOnly + vbExclamation + vbDefaultButton1    ' Define buttons.
Title = "ERROR Check"    ' Define title.
Response = MsgBox(Msg, Style, Title)
    
    If Response = vbOK Then    ' User chose OK.

    Form_DIM_TEST_10.EMP_ID.Value = ""
    Form_DIM_TEST_10.EMP_ID.SetFocus

    End If

Else

Form_DIM_TEST_10.TEST_DATE.SetFocus
Form_DIM_TEST_10.TEST_DATE.Value = Date

Form_DIM_TEST_10.MOLD_DATE.SetFocus
Form_DIM_TEST_10.MOLD_DATE.Value = Date


TestDate1 = Form_DIM_TEST_10.TEST_DATE.Value
EmpID1 = Form_DIM_TEST_10.EMP_ID.Value

Form_DIM_TEST_10.EMP_NAME_Label.Visible = True
Form_DIM_TEST_10.EMP_NAME.Visible = True
Form_DIM_TEST_10.EMP_NAME.SetFocus
Form_DIM_TEST_10.EMP_NAME.Value = EmpName1

Form_DIM_TEST_10.PartNo.SetFocus

Form_DIM_TEST_10.EMP_ID_Label.Visible = False
Form_DIM_TEST_10.EMP_ID.Visible = False

End If

End Sub

End Sub

Private Sub MOLD_NO_AfterUpdate()
With CodeContextObject
.[Cavs] = .[MOLD_NO].Column(1)

Form_DIM_TEST_10.ResinNo.SetFocus
End With
End Sub

With CodeContextObject
.[MOLD_NO].Requery

Form_DIM_TEST_10.MOLD_NO.SetFocus
End With
End Sub

Private Sub TestName_AfterUpdate()
With CodeContextObject

TestColumn = 0
Test_Order_EM = 0
Test_Order_MAR = 0

Call ClearForm

' ************** Set Header information **********************

If DLookup("[TestType]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 1") <> "" Then
Form_DIM_TEST_10.lblT1.Caption = DLookup("[TestType]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 1")
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T1Max.SetFocus
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T1Max.Value = DLookup("[TestHighLim]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 1")

Form_DIM_TEST_10.T1Min.SetFocus
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T1Min.Value = DLookup("[TestLowLim]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 1")
        TestColumn = 1
End If

If DLookup("[TestType]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 2") <> "" Then
Form_DIM_TEST_10.lblT2.Caption = DLookup("[TestType]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 2")
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T2Max.SetFocus
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T2Max.Value = DLookup("[TestHighLim]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 2")

Form_DIM_TEST_10.T2Min.SetFocus
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T2Min.Value = DLookup("[TestLowLim]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 2")
        TestColumn = TestColumn + 1
    
    If DLookup("[TestEM]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 2") = 1 And DLookup("[TestMAR]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 2") = 0 Then
        Test_Order_EM = 2
        TestColumn = TestColumn - 1
    End If
    If DLookup("[TestEM]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 2") = 1 And DLookup("[TestMAR]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 2") = 1 Then
        Test_Order_MAR = 2
        TestColumn = TestColumn - 1
        Form_DIM_TEST_10.T2Max.SetFocus
        Form_DIM_TEST_10.T2Max.Value = DLookup("[TestAccept]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 2")
        
        Forms![DIM_TEST_10]![TAR2] = -1
        
        Form_DIM_TEST_10.T2Min.SetFocus
        Form_DIM_TEST_10.T2Min.Value = DLookup("[TestReject]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 2")
    End If
End If

If DLookup("[TestType]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 3") <> "" Then
Form_DIM_TEST_10.lblT3.Caption = DLookup("[TestType]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 3")
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T3Max.SetFocus
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T3Max.Value = DLookup("[TestHighLim]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 3")

Form_DIM_TEST_10.T3Min.SetFocus
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T3Min.Value = DLookup("[TestLowLim]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 3")
        TestColumn = TestColumn + 1
    
    If DLookup("[TestEM]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 3") = 1 And DLookup("[TestMAR]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 3") = 0 Then
        Test_Order_EM = 3
        TestColumn = TestColumn - 1
    End If
    If DLookup("[TestEM]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 3") = 1 And DLookup("[TestMAR]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 3") = 1 Then
        Test_Order_MAR = 3
        TestColumn = TestColumn - 1
        Form_DIM_TEST_10.T3Max.SetFocus
        Form_DIM_TEST_10.T3Max.Value = DLookup("[TestAccept]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 3")
        
        Forms![DIM_TEST_10]![TAR3] = -1

        Form_DIM_TEST_10.T3Min.SetFocus
        Form_DIM_TEST_10.T3Min.Value = DLookup("[TestReject]", "TestCriteria", "[TestName] = '" & Forms!DIM_TEST_10!TestName & "' And [TestOrder] = 3")

Private Sub Col1ReCalc()

Dim LoopCounter
Dim CalcCount
SV01Max = 0
SV01Min = 1000
SV01Tot = 0
CalcCount = 0

For LoopCounter = 1 To 140

    If (ReadingValue(1, LoopCounter) <> "") Then
        If ReadingValue(1, LoopCounter) >= SV01Max Then
            SV01Max = ReadingValue(1, LoopCounter)
        End If
        If ReadingValue(1, LoopCounter) <= SV01Min Then
            SV01Min = ReadingValue(1, LoopCounter)
        End If
    SV01Tot = SV01Tot + ReadingValue(1, LoopCounter)
    CalcCount = CalcCount + 1
    End If

Next

If SV01Max <> 0 Then
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T1HI.Value = SV01Max
End If
If SV01Min <> 1000 Then
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T1LOW.Value = SV01Min
End If
If SV01Tot <> 0 And CalcCount <> 0 Then
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T1AVG.Value = Round((SV01Tot / CalcCount), 4)
End If

End Sub

Private Sub Col7ReCalc()

Dim LoopCounter
Dim CalcCount
SV07Max = 0
SV07Min = 1000
SV07Tot = 0
CalcCount = 0

For LoopCounter = 1 To 140

    If (ReadingValue(7, LoopCounter) <> "") Then
        If ReadingValue(7, LoopCounter) >= SV07Max Then
            SV07Max = ReadingValue(7, LoopCounter)
        End If
        If ReadingValue(7, LoopCounter) <= SV07Min Then
            SV07Min = ReadingValue(7, LoopCounter)
        End If
    SV07Tot = SV07Tot + ReadingValue(7, LoopCounter)
    CalcCount = CalcCount + 1
    End If

Next

If SV07Max <> 0 Then
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T7HI.Value = SV07Max
End If
If SV07Min <> 1000 Then
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T7LOW.Value = SV07Min
End If
If SV07Tot <> 0 And CalcCount <> 0 Then
Form_DIM_TEST_10.T7AVG.Value = Round((SV07Tot / CalcCount), 4)
End If

End Sub
